       <tr> 
        <td class="intro"><p><strong>University of California Riverside to Launch Ph.D. in Art History in Fall 2014<br /> </strong><br /> Expanding its graduate programs, the University of California, Riverside will offer a Ph.D. in art history beginning in fall 2014.&nbsp;The doctoral program will offer interdisciplinary training across the history of art, with special strengths in the history of photography, sculpture and architecture.&nbsp;The program will be small, intensive, and committed to producing scholars who take a global, interdisciplinary approach to the history of the visual arts.<br /> </p></td>

     <div class="row"> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <h1 class="page-header">Alumni and Constituent Affairs</h1> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span12"> 
       <ul class="nav nav-tabs sub-nav tab4"> 
        <li class="active"><a class="" href="index.html">Overview</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="staff-contacts/index.html">Staff &amp; Contacts</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="services-programs/index.html">Services &amp; programs</a></li> 
        <li class=""><a class="" href="support-uc/index.html">Support UC</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <!-- Example row of columns --> 
     <div class="row-fluid"> 
      <div class="span4 hero-unit"> 
       <p>We help alumni help UC.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="span4">
       <p>UC has more than 1.6 million alumni living and working around the globe. They are leaders and contributors to the vitality of our communities, our businesses and our culture. The mission of the Alumni and Constituent Affairs office is to enrich the lives of alumni and engage them as volunteers, advocates and contributors who strengthen the University of California.</p>
      </div> 
      <div class="span4"> 
       <div class="row-fluid dotted-bottom"> 
        <div class="span4 dept-head"> 
         <img alt="John Valva" src="_images/shot_17_jvalva_022 2.jpg" />
        </div> 
        <div class="span8"> 
         <p class="blue"> John Valva </p> 
         <p>Executive Director</p> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
       <div class="row-fluid"> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon staff" href="staff-contacts/index.html">Staff Directory</a>
        </div> 
        <div class="span6"> 
         <a class="icon org" href="_files/Alumni_org_chart_11-28-12.pdf">Org Chart</a>
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div>

    var ytpreload = ytpreload || {};
    ytpreload.SnapClassList = ['content-snap-width-1', 'content-snap-width-2',
                               'content-snap-width-3'];
    ytpreload.getSnapClass = function(guidePinned) {
      var SCROLLBAR_WIDTH = 21;
      var CONTENT_PADDING = 50;
      var GUIDE_WIDTH = 230;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_2 = 1056;
      var SNAP_WIDTH_3 = 1262;
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;

      var spaceForContent = screenWidth - SCROLLBAR_WIDTH - CONTENT_PADDING;
      if (ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle() && guidePinned) {
        spaceForContent -= GUIDE_WIDTH;
      }

      if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_3) {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[2];
      } else if (spaceForContent >= SNAP_WIDTH_2){
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[1];
      } else {
        return ytpreload.SnapClassList[0];
      }

    };
    ytpreload.GUIDE_PINNED_CLASS = 'guide-pinned';
    ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS = 'show-guide';
    ytpreload.usePinnedGuideStyle = function() {
      var screenWidth = window.innerWidth ||
          document.documentElement.clientWidth;
      return screenWidth >= 1251;
    };

            classList.push(ytpreload.GUIDE_VISIBILITY_CLASS);
        }
        classList.push(' ', ytpreload.getSnapClass(
            true));
      htmlEl.className = classList.join(' ');
    })();

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <img src="/Images/special-programs.png" alt="" class="page-lead" /> 
     <div class="span-8"> 
      <h3>Earn Credit Off-Campus</h3> 
      <p>UCR students are innovative learners. We give credit for work completed in unique circumstances. Certain procedures must be followed and only specific programs qualify. Military programs, extension courses and studying abroad are just some of the ways you can earn credit for extraordinary work. </p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-10 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar" style="margin-left: 0px;"> 
       <span class="warning">Important</span> 
       <img style="float: right;" src="../../Images/paperpushpin.png" alt="" /> 
       <ul> 
        <li>Consult with your academic advisor if you want to earn credit through an off-campus class. </li> 
        <li>Dean pre-approval is required for most off-campus coursework. </li> 
        <li>The <a href="http://www.assist.org/web-assist/welcome.html">ASSIST</a> website is another good resource for up-to-date information on transfer credit earned at California public colleges and universities.</li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <br /> 
     <br /> 
     <div class="span-18 last"> 
      <div class="padding"> 
       <div class="tabs"> 
        <table class="tabs gray"> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td class="selected" id="tab1">Summer Classes</td> 
           <td id="tab2">UCR Extension</td> 
           <td id="tab3">Cross Registration Programs</td> 
           <td id="tab4">Internships</td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>
        </table> 
        <table class="nav gray"> 
         <tbody>
          <tr> 
           <td colspan="4"></td> 
          </tr> 
         </tbody>
        </table> 
       </div> 
       <div class="tab-content"> 
        <div id="tab1-content"> 
         <h4>UCR and Off-Campus Summer Classes</h4> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
          <li> <p> Credit earned through UCR Summer Session classes will automatically appear on your academic record. </p> </li> 
          <li> <p> If you want to earn credit by taking a summer class at another school (including another UC), you must get the course work pre-approved by the dean of your college. </p> </li> 
          <li> <p> To earn credit for approved coursework taken on another campus, you must submit that transcript to <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/meetCounselor">Undergraduate Admissions</a>. </p> </li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <div id="tab2-content" class="hide"> 
         <h4>UCR Extension</h4> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
          <li> <p> Only courses in UCR Extensions concurrent enrollment program are transferable and count toward your UCR degree. </p> </li> 
          <li> <p> Extension credit will not automatically appear on your academic record. You must submit an Extension transcript to <a href="http://admissions.ucr.edu/Admissions/meetCounselor">Undergraduate Admissions</a>. </p> </li> 
          <li> <p> If you are attending UCR Extension because you were dismissed from UCR, you may need to get additional approval and signatures before you can earn transferable credit. </p> </li> 
          <li> <p> Please contact <a href="http://www.extension.ucr.edu">UCR Extension</a> with questions. </p> </li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <div id="tab3-content" class="hide"> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
          <li> <strong>Air Force Reserve Officer Training Corps (AFROTC)</strong><br /> <p> <a href="http://afrotc.csusb.edu/" target="_blank">AFROTC</a> participants train to become United States Air Force second lieutenants while completing their degree and may enroll in classes at California State University, San Bernardino. Call (909) 537-5440 for details. </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Army ROTC (AROTC)</strong><br /> <p> Two and four-year AROTC programs are available through an agreement with<a href="http://www.goarmy.com/rotc/schools/claremont-mckenna-college.html" target="_blank"> Claremont McKenna College</a> and the <a href="http://armyrotc.csusb.edu/" target="_blank">Department of Military Science at California State University, San Bernardino</a>. Participants may earn elective credit toward their UCR degree. Successful completion results in a commission as a second lieutenant with subsequent service in the Army Reserve or National Guard. Call (909) 537-5533 (or 5534) for details. </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Reserve Officers Training Corps</strong> <p> With dean approval, students may enroll in ROTC courses at another institution while completing their degree at UCR. Students interested in Air Force ROTC should contact Admissions at (951) 827-3411. Those interested in Army ROTC should contact our special programs coordinator at (951) 827-3409. Program pamphlets are also available at the <a href="http://careers.ucr.edu/Pages/default.aspx">Career Center.</a> </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Education Abroad Program (EAP)</strong> <p> EAP gives UC students the opportunity to grow as global citizens while earning UC credit. It has study abroad programs in 36+ countries at the some of the finest universities in the world. Please contact <a href="http://eapoap.ucr.edu">EAP</a> for details. </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Intercampus Visitor Program (ICV)</strong> <p> The ICV program is good for those who want to take an entire quarter of classes at another UC campus. Qualified participants can take classes unavailable at UCR, participate in unique programs or study with a specific faculty member. Students may enroll at another UC campus for only one term. Go to the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS), on the first floor of the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=SSB">Student Services Building</a>, for additional information and an application. </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Simultaneous Enrollment and Cross-Campus Enrollment</strong> <p style="margin-bottom: 8px;">Simultaneous Enrollment is similar to the ICV, but participants are enrolled in at least six units at UCR while simultaneously taking additional classes at another UC campus.&nbsp; Cross-Campus Enrollment allows participants to simultaneously take online courses offered by another UC campus.&nbsp; Participants of either program dont have to be formally admitted nor pay additional tuition/fees; however other fees may apply depending on the course. For additional information and application for Simultaneous Enrollment, please go to the Highlander One Stop Shop (HOSS), on the first floor of the <a href="http://campusmap.ucr.edu/imap/index.html?loc=SSB">Student Services Building</a>.&nbsp; For additional information and to initiate enrollment for Cross-Campus Enrollment course opportunities please go to <a href="http://crossenroll.universityofcalifornia.edu">crossenroll.universityofcalifornia.edu</a>.&nbsp;</p> <p>Eligibility requirements for both programs include:</p> 
           <ul style="margin-bottom: 10px;"> 
            <li>Has completed a minimum of 12 units as a matriculated student at UCR (home campus).</li> 
            <li>Is enrolled for a minimum of 6 units for the current term at UCR (home campus)</li> 
            <li>Is in good standing.</li> 
            <li>Has the appropriate academic preparation as determined by the host campus.</li> 
            <li>Must have fees paid by Fee Payment deadline. </li> 
           </ul> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Senate Bill 1914 (Killea)</strong> <p> Killea lets undergraduate students enrolled in any California community college, California State University or UC to enroll without formal admission in one course for one term at another campus within those three systems. This happens on a space-available basis and at the discretion of campus authorities. Contact us for program details and requirements. </p> </li> 
          <li> <strong>Cal State San Bernardino Cross-Registration Program</strong> <p> This program allows full-time UCR undergraduate students (who have declared a major and are in good academic standing) to enroll at CSSB for one course per quarter. Approvals are required ahead of time from your academic advisor, college dean and <a href="/registrar/help-desk/about-us.aspx">our office</a>. We can also give you application forms and deadline information. Please note: this program is not available during summer session! </p> </li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
        <div id="tab4-content" class="hide"> 
         <h4>Internships </h4> 
         <p>If you are curious about internships, or want to know if you can earn credit for a particular one, please contact the <a href="http://www.careers.ucr.edu/Pages/default.aspx">Career Center.</a> </p> 
         <p> <a href="/registrar/help-desk/about-us.aspx">Contact us</a> to learn more about these two standout internship programs: </p> 
         <ul class="orange-bullets"> 
          <li> <h4 class="shadow"><strong><a href="http://www.ucdc.ucr.edu/" target="_blank">UCR Washington Academic Internship Program</a></strong></h4> UCR Director: Thomas M. Perring, Ph.D.<br /> UCR Coordinators: Trina Elerts (campus) &amp; Chantal Quintero (DC)<br /> Undergraduate Education<br /> 2319 Olmsted Hall<br /> <br /> </li> 
          <li><strong><a href="http://admissions.ucdavis.edu/careerprep/sacramento_program.cfm" target="_blank">UC Center Sacramento Scholar Intern Program</a></strong> <br /> <br /> Associate Director and Public Affairs Journalism Director: AG Block<br /> 1130 K Street, Suite LL22<br /> Sacramento, CA 95814<br /> (916) 445-5100 or (951) 827-2634<br /> </li> 
         </ul> 
        </div> 
       </div> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
    </div>

  <div class="pagewrapper"> 
   <h3 class="accessibility">Footer</h3> 
   <div id="colophon">
     The University of California, Riverside (
    <a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR's enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus opened a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. A broadcast studio with fiber cable to the AT&amp;T Hollywood hub is available for live or taped interviews. UCR also has ISDN for radio interviews. To learn more, call (951) UCR-NEWS. 
   </div>
